=== Didascalia ===

=== Akt II ===

(999a) [CHARINUS ADULESCENS:] thus thing|matter is. daughter to|you my Philumena
(1000a) [CHREMES SENEX:] uxōrem(A) et(Kon) dōtis(G) sex(Adj) talenta(A) spondeō(Prä)(Akt).
(1000a) [CHREMES SENEX:] as|wife and of|dowry six talents I|promise.
